I was just so excited reading all the positive reviews and the stating of it being \\"all-natural\\" - dumb me..<br /><br />Unfortunately, the product contains Phenoxyethanol, which can be very irritating to the skin and is proven toxic if the content is more than 1% of the product. It is hard to determine what percentage that is used in this product. Ingredients are listed in descending order and it is listed as the second to last ingredient. However, it also depends on how much you use the product to go over that 1% safe point. It's scary because Phenoxyethanol has been banned in the use of cosmetics in many countries because of its risk.<br /><br />When parabens became a hot topic, cosmetic industries scrambled to find an alternative, Phenoxyethanol became the quick-fix, but there are far better and safer preservatives out there. This product also uses Caprylyl Glycol as a preservative which has no toxicity level, which is GREAT! However, I wish this formula would be changed to utilize Potassium Sorbate w/citric acid combined with the Caprylyl Glycol, or by using Naticide or Leucidal as the only preservative.<br /><br />However, I will give it a try and use it minimally as that is the safest route! :)<br /><br />If I find that it works and doesn't cause any irritation or dryness, that will be one very good indicator of it not being a high percentage of Phenoxyethanol, and I will come back and change my review.
